# Lightrail Public API Specification
Lightrail Public API Specification

## Version: 0.0.1

### Available authorizations
#### BearerAuth (HTTP, bearer)
Bearer format: JWT

---
## info
Shared infrastructure and health monitoring operations for the Lightrail platform.

Provides essential system health checks and common utilities that support all domain operations across the API.

### [GET] /health
**Check API Health Status**

Checks the overall health and availability of the Lightrail API platform.

The endpoint requires no authentication and responds with the current service status and availability information.

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Successful health check response indicating API availability.  Confirms that the API is operational and ready to process requests. Used by load balancers, monitoring systems, and client applications to verify service availability. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [Health](#health)<br> |
| 429 | Rate limiting error indicating too many requests from the client.  Returned when the request frequency exceeds the allowed rate limits. Clients should implement exponential backoff and retry logic. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 500 | Server error indicating an unexpected failure in request processing.  Returned when an internal system error occurs. Include the Request-Id when reporting these errors for faster resolution. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |

---
## account_access
Role-based access control (RBAC) APIs for managing account permissions and user access.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/roles
**List Account Roles**

Retrieves all roles configured for the specified account, including both directly assigned and inherited roles.

Returns comprehensive role information showing:
- Assigned roles: Roles directly configured on this account
- Inherited roles: Roles inherited from parent accounts in the hierarchy

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Account roles retrieved successfully<br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [GetAccountRolesSuccessBody](#getaccountrolessuccessbody)<br> |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation.  Returned when the authenticated user lacks the necessary roles or permissions to access the specified resource or perform the requested action. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 404 | Resource not found error indicating the requested entity does not exist.  Returned when the specified resource identifier (account, order, product, etc.) cannot be located or has been deleted. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 422 | Business logic validation failure where the request is well-formed but cannot be processed.  Returned when the request data is valid but violates business rules, such as insufficient funds, quota limits, or operational constraints. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 429 | Rate limiting error indicating too many requests from the client.  Returned when the request frequency exceeds the allowed rate limits. Clients should implement exponential backoff and retry logic. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 500 | Server error indicating an unexpected failure in request processing.  Returned when an internal system error occurs. Include the Request-Id when reporting these errors for faster resolution. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |

| Security Schema | Scopes |
| --------------- | ------ |
| BearerAuth |  |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/roles/{role_name}/members
**Assign Actor to Role**

Assigns an actor (user or API client) to a specific role within the account, granting all associated permissions.

Actors (users or API clients) gain access to operations based on their role assignments. This endpoint:
- Grants the actor all permissions associated with the specified role
- Enables inheritance of role-based access to child accounts
- Supports both individual users and programmatic API clients

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| role_name | path | Name of the role to operate on within the account.  Role names identify specific permission containers and must match existing roles configured for the account. Use the List Account Roles endpoint to discover available role names.  | Yes | [AccountRole](#accountrole) |

#### Request Body

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [AddActorToRoleRequestBody](#addactortorolerequestbody)<br> |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> |  |
| 204 | Actor successfully added to role<br>**Headers:**<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> |  |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation.  Returned when the authenticated user lacks the necessary roles or permissions to access the specified resource or perform the requested action. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 404 | Resource not found error indicating the requested entity does not exist.  Returned when the specified resource identifier (account, order, product, etc.) cannot be located or has been deleted. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 422 | Business logic validation failure where the request is well-formed but cannot be processed.  Returned when the request data is valid but violates business rules, such as insufficient funds, quota limits, or operational constraints. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 429 | Rate limiting error indicating too many requests from the client.  Returned when the request frequency exceeds the allowed rate limits. Clients should implement exponential backoff and retry logic. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/roles/{role_name}/members
**List Role Members**

Retrieves all users and API clients assigned to a specific role within the account.

Returns detailed membership information including:
- Assigned members: Users directly assigned to this role on this account
- Inherited members: Users who have this role through parent account inheritance

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| role_name | path | Name of the role to operate on within the account.  Role names identify specific permission containers and must match existing roles configured for the account. Use the List Account Roles endpoint to discover available role names.  | Yes | [AccountRole](#accountrole) |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Role members retrieved successfully<br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [GetRoleMembersSuccessBody](#getrolememberssuccessbody)<br> |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation.  Returned when the authenticated user lacks the necessary roles or permissions to access the specified resource or perform the requested action. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |

Returned when the specified resource identifier (account, order, product, etc.) cannot be located or has been deleted. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 422 | Business logic validation failure where the request is well-formed but cannot be processed.  Returned when the request data is valid but violates business rules, such as insufficient funds, quota limits, or operational constraints. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/roles/{role_name}/members/{actor_id}
**Unassign User from Role**

Removes an actor (user or API client) from a specific role within the account, revoking associated permissions.

This operation will:
- Remove the actor's assignment to the specified role
- Revoke all permissions granted through this role, except inherited ones
- Maintain any other role assignments the actor may have

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| role_name | path | Name of the role to operate on within the account.  Role names identify specific permission containers and must match existing roles configured for the account. Use the List Account Roles endpoint to discover available role names.  | Yes | [AccountRole](#accountrole) |
| actor_id | path | Unique identifier for an actor (user or API client) within your organization.  Actor IDs represent both human users and programmatic API clients that can be assigned to roles. Use the List Role Members endpoint to discover actor IDs assigned to specific roles.  | Yes | string |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> |  |
| 204 | Actor successfully removed from role<br>**Headers:**<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> |  |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation.  Returned when the authenticated user lacks the necessary roles or permissions to access the specified resource or perform the requested action. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 404 | Resource not found error indicating the requested entity does not exist. Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 422 | Business logic validation failure where the request is well-formed but cannot be processed.  Returned when the request data is valid but violates business rules, such as insufficient funds, quota limits, or operational constraints. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/roles/{role_name}/permissions
**List Role Permissions**

Retrieves all permissions assigned to a specific role within the account, showing both direct and inherited permissions.

Returns comprehensive permission information including:
- Assigned permissions: Permissions directly granted to this role on this account
- Inherited permissions: Permissions inherited from parent accounts for this role

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| role_name | path | Name of the role to operate on within the account.  Role names identify specific permission containers and must match existing roles configured for the account. Use the List Account Roles endpoint to discover available role names.  | Yes | [AccountRole](#accountrole) |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Role permissions retrieved successfully<br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [GetRolePermissionsSuccessBody](#getrolepermissionssuccessbody)<br> |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation. ### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/access
**Retrieve Account Access Configuration**

Retrieves the complete access control configuration for the specified account, including applied, inherited, and resolved permissions.

Returns comprehensive access information showing:
- Applied access control: Roles and permissions directly configured on this account
- Inherited access control: Roles and permissions inherited from parent accounts
- Resolved access control: Final effective permissions combining applied and inherited settings

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/members
**List Account Members**

Retrieves all actors (users and API clients) with access to the specified account, including their role assignments and inheritance information.

Returns comprehensive member information showing:
- Actor details: User or API client identification and contact information
- Role assignments: All roles assigned to each actor, including inherited roles
- Inheritance details: Source account for inherited role assignments
- Organization admin status: Whether the actor has organization-level administrative privileges

Use the type query parameter to filter results by actor type (all, members, or api_clients).

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| type | query | Type of actors to return in the response.  Filters the results to include only the specified actor type: - `all`: Returns both users and API clients (default) - `members`: Returns only user actors - `api_clients`: Returns only API client actors  | No | string, <br>**Available values:** "all", "members", "api_clients", <br>**Default:** all |

## transactions
Comprehensive transaction tracking and financial audit trail management for all account operations.

Provides complete visibility into financial movements including transfers, balance adjustments, order payments, and payout redemptions with detailed categorization and compliance reporting.

### [GET] /organizations/{org_id}/transactions
**List Organization Transaction History**

Retrieves comprehensive transaction history across all accounts within an organization for financial oversight and compliance reporting.

Returns detailed transaction records for all organizational accounts including transfers, adjustments, orders, and payouts. Essential for financial reconciliation, audit compliance, and cross-account analysis.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| org_id | path | Unique identifier for the organization.  Organization IDs scope operations to specific organizational contexts and ensure proper data isolation between different business entities using the platform.  | Yes | string |
| start_date | query | Filter records newer than this date (inclusive) | No | dateTime |
| end_date | query | Filter records older than this date (exclusive) | No | dateTime |
| limit | query | Maximum number of items to return in a single page of results in a paginated response.  | No | integer, <br>**Default:** 50 |
| offset | query | Number of items to skip from the beginning of the result set in a paginated response.  | No | integer |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Transactions retrieved successfully<br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

## accounts
Core account management for creating, configuring, and maintaining customer accounts within organizational hierarchies.

Provides comprehensive account lifecycle management including creation, updates, balance management, and hierarchical organization for financial services and payouts program operations.

### [POST] /accounts
**Create Customer Account**

Creates a new customer account within the organizational hierarchy with configurable settings and permissions.

Accounts serve as the primary entity for managing customer relationships, financial balances, and access controls. They support hierarchical organization for businesses managing multiple customer segments or subsidiaries.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |

#### Request Body

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [CreateAccountRequestBody](#createaccountrequestbody)<br> |

## account_balance

## orders
Order processing and fulfillment management for digital product purchases and payout distribution.

Comprehensive order lifecycle management including creation, payment processing, fulfillment tracking, and delivery confirmation for digital products and services.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/orders
**List Account Order History**

Retrieves comprehensive order history for an account with advanced filtering capabilities for customer service and account management.

Returns detailed order information including status, fulfillment details, payment information, and associated digital products. Supports pagination and date range filtering for efficient data access.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| start_date | query | Filter records newer than this date (inclusive) | No | dateTime |
| end_date | query | Filter records older than this date (exclusive) | No | dateTime |
| limit | query | Maximum number of items to return in a single page of results in a paginated response.  | No | integer, <br>**Default:** 50 |
| offset | query | Number of items to skip from the beginning of the result set in a paginated response.  | No | integer |

---
## payouts
Digital payout creation and management for distributing payouts, gift cards, and monetary benefits to customers.

Provides comprehensive payout lifecycle management including creation, fulfillment tracking, expiration management, and secure distribution through multiple channels including email, SMS, and direct links.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/payouts
**List Account Payout History**

Retrieves comprehensive payout history for a specific customer account with filtering capabilities for payout management and customer service.

Returns detailed payout information including status, claim activity, expiration dates, and fulfillment details. Essential for customer support, payout tracking, and payout lifecycle management.

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |

| start_date | query | Filter records newer than this date (inclusive) | No | dateTime |
| end_date | query | Filter records older than this date (exclusive) | No | dateTime |
| limit | query | Maximum number of items to return in a single page of results in a paginated response.  | No | integer, <br>**Default:** 50 |
| offset | query | Number of items to skip from the beginning of the result set in a paginated response.  | No | integer |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/payouts/{payout_id}/flags
**Set Payout Configuration Flag**

Sets a configuration flag for a specific payout to control its behavior, security settings, or operational status.

Enables payout management including activation/deactivation, security controls, and administrative actions.

This operation is idempotent - setting an already active flag returns 204 without error.

### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/payouts/{payout_id}/flags/{flag}
**Remove Payout Configuration Flag**

Removes a specific configuration flag from a payout, reverting to default behavior or clearing operational states.

Enables payout management flexibility by removing flag-based controls.

This operation is idempotent - removing a non-existent flag returns 204 without error.

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |

---
## payout_links
Secure payout link generation and management for customer self-service claim and digital distribution.

Enables creation of secure, tokenized links that customers can use to claim their payouts. Supports customizable claim experiences, security controls, and comprehensive usage analytics.

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/payouts/{payout_id}/links
**Generate Secure Payout Link**

Generates a secure, shareable link that enables customers to access and claim their payout without requiring authentication.

Payout links provide a seamless customer experience for digital payout distribution through email, SMS, or direct sharing. Each link includes configurable security controls and expiration settings.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| payout_id | path | Unique identifier for the payout.  Payout IDs reference specific reward distributions and enable tracking of fulfillment status, claim activity, and customer engagement metrics.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 201 | Payout link created successfully<br>**Headers:**<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [PayoutLinkInfo](#payoutlinkinfo)<br> |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> |  |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

---
## auth
API client authentication and programmatic access management for your organization

### [GET] /auth/clients
**List Organization API Clients**

Retrieves all API clients created within your organization for programmatic access to the Lightrail API.

API clients enable secure machine-to-machine communication and are ideal for:
- Server-side applications and services
- Automated reward processing systems
- Integration with existing business systems
- Scheduled operations and batch processing

Each client includes configuration details and settings, but excludes sensitive information like client secrets for security.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| cursor | query | Cursor token for retrieving the prev/next page of results in paginated responses.  Use the cursor value returned in the previous response to fetch subsequent pages. Cursor-based pagination provides consistent results even when the underlying data changes.  | No | string |
| limit | query | Maximum number of items to return in a single page of results in a paginated response.  | No | integer, <br>**Default:** 50 |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 200 | Successful response containing paginated list of API clients for your organization.  Results are ordered by creation date (newest first) and include client metadata but exclude sensitive information like client secrets. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: { **"items"**: [ [GetAPIClientSuccessBody](#getapiclientsuccessbody) ], **"next_cursor"**: string, **"total"**: integer }<br> |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure.  Common causes include missing required fields, invalid data types, malformed JSON, or parameter values that don't meet validation requirements. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 401 | Authentication failure due to missing, invalid, or expired credentials.  Returned when the request lacks valid authentication credentials or the provided JWT token is invalid, expired, or malformed. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> | **application/json**: [APIResponseError](#apiresponseerror)<br> |
| 403 | Authorization failure indicating insufficient permissions for the requested operation. ### [POST] /auth/clients
**Create API Client**

Creates a new API client for programmatic access to the Lightrail API.

API clients provide secure authentication for applications and services that need to interact with Lightrail. Use this endpoint to:
- Set up new integrations with business systems
- Create dedicated clients for different environments (development, staging, production)
- Configure specific permission levels for different use cases
- Enable automated reward processing workflows

The response includes the client secret which is only shown once during creation. Store this securely as it cannot be retrieved later.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |

#### Request Body

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [CreateAPIClientRequestBody](#createapiclientrequestbody)<br> |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |

### [DELETE] /auth/clients/{client_id}
**Delete API Client**

Permanently removes an API client and revokes all associated authentication tokens.

Use this endpoint to:
- Decommission outdated integrations
- Remove compromised clients
- Clean up unused or test clients
- Revoke access for terminated services

Warning: This action immediately invalidates all tokens issued to this client and cannot be undone. Ensure all dependent systems are updated before deletion.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| client_id | path | Unique identifier for an API client within your organization.  This ID is returned when creating an API client and is used to reference the client in management operations.  | Yes | string |

### [POST] /auth/authenticate
**Authenticate API Client**

Exchanges API client credentials for a JWT access token to authenticate API requests.

This endpoint is the entry point for all programmatic API access. Use it to:
- Obtain access tokens for API requests
- Authenticate server-side applications
- Enable automated system integrations
- Implement secure machine-to-machine communication

The returned JWT token should be included in the Authorization header as a Bearer token for all subsequent API calls. 
Tokens have a limited lifetime of 1 hour and should be refreshed before expiration.

#### Request Body

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [AuthenticateAPIClientRequestBody](#authenticateapiclientrequestbody)<br> |

---
## account_catalog
Account-specific catalog configuration and product visibility management.

Enables granular control over product availability through inheritance-based visibility rules, exclusions, inclusions, and program associations within account hierarchies.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/overrides
**Get Account Catalog Configuration**

Retrieves comprehensive catalog configuration for an account including both assigned and inherited settings.

Returns detailed visibility into account-specific catalog overrides including:
- **Product Visibility**: Show/hide configurations for specific products
- **Child Account Rules**: Inclusion and exclusion lists inherited by child accounts
- **Program Associations**: Customer program assignments affecting product availability
- **Inheritance Chain**: Both directly assigned and inherited configurations from parent accounts

The response provides complete transparency into how catalog visibility is resolved within the account hierarchy.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/overrides
**Configure Account Catalog Settings**

Configures comprehensive catalog visibility and inheritance rules for an account.

Enables detailed control over product availability through multiple configuration layers:
- **Product Visibility**: Define which products are shown or hidden in this account's catalog
- **Child Account Inheritance**: Set inclusion and exclusion rules that child accounts will inherit
- **Program Assignment**: Associate customer programs that affect product availability
- **Hierarchical Rules**: Override inherited settings while maintaining parent-child relationships

Changes are applied immediately and cascade to child accounts according to inheritance rules. The operation is idempotent and safe to retry.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/exclusions/{shortcode}
**Exclude Product from Child Account Catalogs**

Adds a product to the exclusion list, preventing child accounts from accessing it in their catalogs.

This hierarchical control mechanism ensures child accounts cannot see or order the specified product, regardless of other visibility settings. The exclusion cascades through the account hierarchy, affecting all descendant accounts.

Use this endpoint to implement product restrictions, compliance requirements, or business rules that prevent specific products from being available to subsidiary accounts.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| shortcode | path | Product shortcode serving as the primary identifier for catalog products.  Human-readable identifier used consistently across the platform for product reference, visibility management, and approval workflows.  | Yes | string |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br> |  |
| 204 | Product successfully added to list of excluded products, not available for children accounts<br>**Headers:**<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.
<br> |  |
| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure. ### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/exclusions/{shortcode}
**Remove Product from Child Account Exclusions**

Removes a product from the exclusion list, allowing child accounts to access it again in their catalogs.

This operation restores product availability to child accounts by removing hierarchical restrictions. Once removed, the product visibility for child accounts will be determined by other catalog configuration rules.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. | shortcode | path | Product shortcode serving as the primary identifier for catalog products.  Human-readable identifier used consistently across the platform for product reference, visibility management, and approval workflows.  | Yes | string |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/inclusions/{shortcode}
**Include Product in Child Account Catalogs**

Adds a product to the inclusion list, ensuring child accounts have access to it in their catalogs.

This creates a whitelist approach where only explicitly included products are available to child accounts. The inclusion cascades through the account hierarchy, making the product accessible to all descendant accounts.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| shortcode | path | Product shortcode serving as the primary identifier for catalog products.  Human-readable identifier used consistently across the platform for product reference, visibility management, and approval workflows.  | Yes | string |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/visible/{shortcode}
**Make Product Visible in Account Catalog**

Adds a product to the account's visible product list, ensuring it appears in this specific account's catalog.

This account-specific visibility control overrides default visibility settings while still respecting parent account exclusion and inclusion rules. The visibility setting only applies to this account and is not inherited by child accounts.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. ### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/visible/{shortcode}
**Remove Product from Account Catalog Visibility**

Removes a product from the account's visible product list, potentially hiding it from this specific account's catalog.

This operation removes the explicit visibility setting for this account. After removal, the product's visibility will be determined by default catalog rules and parent account inheritance settings.

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/hidden/{shortcode}
**Hide Product from Account Catalog**

Adds a product to the account's hidden product list, ensuring it does not appear in this specific account's catalog.

This account-specific visibility control hides products from this account while still respecting parent account exclusion and inclusion rules. The hidden setting only applies to this account and is not inherited by child accounts.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| shortcode | path | Product shortcode serving as the primary identifier for catalog products.  Human-readable identifier used consistently across the platform for product reference, visibility management, and approval workflows.  | Yes | string |

### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/hidden/{shortcode}
**Remove Product from Account Hidden List**

Removes a product from the account's hidden product list, potentially making it visible again in this specific account's catalog.

This operation removes the explicit hiding setting for this account. After removal, the product's visibility will be determined by default catalog rules and parent account inheritance settings.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog
**Get Dynamic Catalog for Account**

Retrieves dynamic catalog results with comprehensive include, exclude, and approval lists for a specific account.

This internal operation processes catalog visibility rules, inheritance settings, and approval requirements to generate a complete catalog view for the account. Returns categorized product lists including included products, excluded products, and products requiring approval workflows.

---
## account_programs
Customer program management and approval program associations.

Enables account-level program assignments and manages the relationship between customer programs and approval requirements for the organization and its accounts.

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/customer-program
**Assign Customer Program to Account**

Associates a customer program identifier with an account's catalog configuration for approval workflow integration.

This assignment links the account to specific approval programs that determine product availability based on brand partnerships and organizational compliance requirements. The program assignment is inheritable by child accounts unless explicitly overridden.

Use this endpoint to establish approval program relationships that control access to restricted or brand-specific products within the catalog hierarchy.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. ### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/catalog/customer-program/{customer_program_id}
**Remove Customer Program from Account**

Removes the customer program association from an account's catalog configuration, affecting approval workflow access.

This operation disconnects the account from the specified approval program, potentially changing product availability based on brand partnerships and compliance requirements. Child accounts may inherit different program settings after this change.

Use this endpoint to revoke approval program relationships when business requirements or compliance status changes.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| customer_program_id | path | Customer program identifier for approval program management and account associations.  Links accounts to specific approval programs that determine product availability based on brand partnerships and organizational compliance requirements.  | Yes | string |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

<br> |  |
| 204 | Customer program ID successfully deleted from catalog configuration<br>**Headers:**<br>**Idempotency-Key**: Echo of the client-provided idempotency key from the request.

Returned in responses to confirm which idempotency key was used for request processing. Helps clients correlate responses with their retry logic.
<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.

| 400 | Client error indicating invalid request format, parameters, or structure. ### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/programs
**List Account Approval Programs**

Retrieves all approval programs available to a specific account based on the resolved customer program identifier.

Returns comprehensive approval program information including:
- **Resolved Program ID**: The effective customer program ID for this account (directly assigned or inherited)
- **Available Programs**: All approval programs accessible based on the resolved program assignment
- **Program Status**: Current approval status and eligibility for brand-specific products

This endpoint provides visibility into which approval programs govern product access for the account within the organizational approval ecosystem.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| limit | query | Maximum number of items to return in a single page of results in a paginated response.  | No | integer, <br>**Default:** 50 |
| offset | query | Number of items to skip from the beginning of the result set in a paginated response.  | No | integer |

---
## account_controls
Financial and operational controls management for account governance, compliance, and risk management.

Provides comprehensive tools for setting spending limits, order restrictions, fee structures, payment method controls, and revenue sharing configurations within your account hierarchy.

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/controls
**Configure Account Controls**

Configures financial and operational controls for an account to ensure governance, compliance, and risk management.

Account controls provide comprehensive oversight capabilities including:
- **Spending Limits**: Daily spend caps and per-order limits to control financial exposure
- **Transfer Controls**: Limits on funds movement between parent and child accounts
- **Payment Configuration**: Approved payment methods and base currency settings
- **Fee Structures**: Fixed and percentage-based order fees for revenue optimization
- **Revenue Sharing**: Margin, fee, and breakage distribution across account hierarchies
- **Default Settings**: Standard order values and operational parameters

All changes are applied immediately and will affect future transactions. This operation is idempotent and safe to retry.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

#### Request Body

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [ControlsConfig](#controlsconfig)<br> |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.

### [GET] /accounts/{account_id}/controls
**Retrieve Account Controls Configuration**

Retrieves the complete controls configuration for an account, including both assigned and inherited settings.

Returns comprehensive control information showing:
- **Assigned Controls**: Controls directly configured on this specific account
- **Inherited Controls**: Controls inherited from parent accounts in the hierarchy
- **Effective Configuration**: The resolved controls that apply to this account

The response provides detailed visibility into all control types including spending limits, transfer restrictions, payment configurations, fee structures, and revenue sharing arrangements that govern account operations.

### [POST] /accounts/{account_id}/flags
**Set Account Configuration Flag**

Sets a configuration flag for a specific customer account to control behavior, security settings, or operational status.

Flags enable flexible account management including activation/deactivation, security controls, feature toggles, and operational status tracking. Changes are audited and can trigger automated business logic.

This operation is idempotent - setting an already active flag returns 204 without error.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |

| Required | Schema |
| -------- | ------ |
|  Yes | **application/json**: [SetFlagRequest](#setflagrequest)<br> |

### [DELETE] /accounts/{account_id}/flags/{flag}
**Remove Account Configuration Flag**

Removes a specific configuration flag from a customer account, reverting to default behavior or inheriting from parent account.

Flag removal enables account management flexibility and allows accounts to inherit settings from parent accounts in the hierarchy. All changes are audited for compliance and operational tracking.

This operation is idempotent - removing a non-existent flag returns 204 without error.

#### Parameters

| Name | Located in | Description | Required | Schema |
| ---- | ---------- | ----------- | -------- | ------ |
| Idempotency-Key | header | Client-generated key to ensure idempotent request processing.  Prevents duplicate operations when the same request is made multiple times. Include this header for all state-changing operations to ensure safe retry behavior and prevent unintended duplicates.  | No | string |
| account_id | path | Unique identifier for an account within your organization's hierarchy.  Account IDs are used consistently across all API operations to reference specific accounts in role assignments, control configurations, and resource management.  | Yes | [UUID](#uuid) |
| flag | path | Flag value on path. Must be one of the AccountFlags values. | Yes | [AccountFlags](#accountflags) |

#### Responses

| Code | Description | Schema |
| ---- | ----------- | ------ |
| 202 | Idempotent request accepted - duplicate processing detected.  Returned when another request with the same idempotency key is currently being processed. The original request is still being handled and will complete normally. <br>**Headers:**<br>**Request-Id**: Unique identifier for tracking and correlating API requests across system logs.

Generated for each API request to enable distributed tracing, debugging, and support case resolution. Include this ID when reporting issues for faster troubleshooting.

### Schemas

#### AccountSettingsName

Identifier for account settings group configurations.

Settings groups define collections of related configuration options that can be applied to accounts. Each group represents a specific operational area or functionality set that can be configured independently.

Settings:
- **onboard_org**: Initial organization setup and configuration

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| AccountSettingsName | string | Identifier for account settings group configurations.  Settings groups define collections of related configuration options that can be applied to accounts. Each group represents a specific operational area or functionality set that can be configured independently.  Settings: - **onboard_org**: Initial organization setup and configuration  |  |

**Example**
<pre>onboard_org</pre>

#### AccountSettingsKind

Category type for hierarchical account settings that can be inherited across account structures.

Settings kinds represent major functional areas of the platform where configurations can be set at parent levels and inherited by child accounts unless explicitly overridden:
- **access**: Role-based permissions and user access controls
- **catalog**: Product visibility and program associations  
- **controls**: Account configuration for financial and operational limits and restrictions

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| AccountSettingsKind | string | Category type for hierarchical account settings that can be inherited across account structures.  Settings kinds represent major functional areas of the platform where configurations can be set at parent levels and inherited by child accounts unless explicitly overridden: - **access**: Role-based permissions and user access controls - **catalog**: Product visibility and program associations   - **controls**: Account configuration for financial and operational limits and restrictions  |  |

**Example**
<pre>access</pre>

#### UUID

Universally unique identifier following RFC 4122 standard.

Used throughout the API to uniquely identify resources such as accounts, orders, products, and other entities. UUIDs ensure global uniqueness and prevent identifier collisions across distributed systems.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| UUID | string | Universally unique identifier following RFC 4122 standard.  Used throughout the API to uniquely identify resources such as accounts, orders, products, and other entities. UUIDs ensure global uniqueness and prevent identifier collisions across distributed systems.  |  |

**Example**
<pre>123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000</pre>

#### PositiveAmountWithCurrency

Monetary amount with associated currency for precise financial calculations.

Combines a decimal amount with its currency code to ensure accurate financial processing across different markets and regions. Used for order values, limits, fees, and all monetary transactions within the platform.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| currency | [Currency](#currency) |  | Yes |
| amount | [PositiveAmountWithoutCurrency](#positiveamountwithoutcurrency) |  | Yes |

**Example**
```<pre>{
  "currency": "USD",
  "amount": "100.00"
}</pre>```

#### AmountWithCurrency

Monetary amount with associated currency for precise financial calculations.

Combines a decimal amount with its currency code to ensure accurate financial processing across different markets and regions. Used for order values, limits, fees, and all monetary transactions within the platform.

| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
