#### AuthPermission

Standardized permission identifiers for auth operations within the Lightrail platform.

These permissions define granular capabilities that can be granted to roles, enabling precise control over what actions actors can perform. 

Group permissions by operational area:

**API Client Management**: create_api_client, update_api_client, delete_api_client, view_org_api_clients, view_all_api_clients

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| AuthPermission | string | Standardized permission identifiers for auth operations within the Lightrail platform.  These permissions define granular capabilities that can be granted to roles, enabling precise control over what actions actors can perform.   Group permissions by operational area:  **API Client Management**: create_api_client, update_api_client, delete_api_client, view_org_api_clients, view_all_api_clients  |  |

**Example**
<pre>create_api_client</pre>

#### CreateAPIClientRequestBody

Request payload for creating a new API client

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| name | string | A unique name for the API client using only alphanumeric characters, hyphens, and underscores.  Choose names that clearly identify the purpose or system using this client. <br>*Example:* `"rewards-processing-service"` | Yes |
| description | string | Optional human-readable description explaining the purpose and usage of this API client.  Include details about the system, environment, or integration this client serves. <br>*Example:* `"Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system"` | No |
| idp_roles | [ [APIActorIdpRole](#apiactoridprole) ] | Array of permission roles to assign to this API client. Roles determine what actions the client can perform.  Most integrations should use 'stytch_member' for standard operations. Only assign 'stytch_admin' when full administrative access is required. <br>*Example:* `["stytch_member"]` | No |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "name": "rewards-processing-service",
  "description": "Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system",
  "idp_roles": [
    "stytch_member"
  ]
}</pre>

#### AuthenticateAPIClientRequestBody

Credentials required to authenticate an API client and receive an access token

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| client_id | string | The unique client identifier returned when the API client was created.  This ID is safe to store in configuration files and logs. <br>*Example:* `"api-client-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"` | Yes |
| client_secret | string | The secret key for this API client. This value is only shown during client creation and cannot be retrieved later. <br>*Example:* `"secret-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"` | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "client_id": "api-client-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
  "client_secret": "secret-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"
}</pre>

#### CreateAPIClientSuccessBody

Response containing the newly created API client details including the client secret

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| client_id | string | Unique identifier for the newly created API client. <br>*Example:* `"api-client-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"` | No |
| client_name | string | The name assigned to the API client<br>*Example:* `"rewards-processing-service"` | No |
| description | string | The description provided for the API client<br>*Example:* `"Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system"` | No |
| client_secret | string | The secret key for this API client. This is the only time this value will be shown.  Store this securely immediately as it cannot be retrieved again. You'll need both the client_id and client_secret to authenticate. <br>*Example:* `"secret-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"` | No |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "client_id": "api-client-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
  "client_name": "rewards-processing-service",
  "description": "Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system",
  "client_secret": "secret-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"
}</pre>

#### GetAPIClientSuccessBody

Response containing API client details and configuration information

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| client_id | string | Unique identifier for the API client. <br>*Example:* `"api-client-7f3c9d8e-4a5b-6c7d-8e9f-0a1b2c3d4e5f"` | No |
| client_name | string | The name assigned to the API client<br>*Example:* `"rewards-processing-service"` | No |
| description | string | The description provided for the API client<br>*Example:* `"Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system"` | No |
| client_secret_last_four | string | Last four characters of the client secret for identification purposes.  The full secret is never returned for security reasons. <br>*Example:* `"4e5f"` | No |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "client_id": "api-client-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
  "client_name": "rewards-processing-service",
  "description": "Production API client for automated gift card ordering and fulfillment system",
  "client_secret_last_four": "4e5f"
}</pre>

#### AuthenticateAPIClientSuccessBody

Response containing a JWT access token for authenticated API requests

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| jwt_token | string | JWT access token for authenticating API requests.  Include this token in the Authorization header as 'Bearer {token}' for all API calls. The token contains your client's identity and permissions. <br>*Example:* `"<your-jwt-token>"` | No |
| expires_in | integer, <br>**Default:** 3600 | Token lifetime in seconds from the time of issue. Plan to refresh the token before this time expires to avoid authentication failures. Default is set to 1 hour. <br>*Example:* `3600` | No |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "jwt_token": "<your-jwt-token>",
  "expires_in": 3600
}</pre>

#### ProductType

Product type classification determining the operational behavior and usage patterns of gift cards and other products.

- **open-loop**: Cards usable at multiple merchants across a payment network (e.g., Visa, Mastercard gift cards)
- **closed-loop**: Cards restricted to specific merchants or brands (e.g., Amazon, Starbucks gift cards)

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| ProductType | string | Product type classification determining the operational behavior and usage patterns of gift cards and other products.  - **open-loop**: Cards usable at multiple merchants across a payment network (e.g., Visa, Mastercard gift cards) - **closed-loop**: Cards restricted to specific merchants or brands (e.g., Amazon, Starbucks gift cards)  |  |

**Example**
<pre>closed-loop</pre>

#### CatalogPermission

Permission constants for account catalog operations and visibility management.

Defines granular access control capabilities for catalog configuration including product visibility, inheritance rules, and program associations. 

These permissions enable role-based access to catalog management functions within account hierarchies.

They are:
- **Catalog Visibility**: Define which products are shown or hidden in this account's catalog: `view_show_in_catalog`, `set_show_in_catalog`, `view_hide_in_catalog`, `set_hide_in_catalog`
- **Child Account Inheritance**: Set inclusion and exclusion rules that child accounts will inherit: `view_excluded_by_parent`, `set_excluded_by_parent`, `view_included_by_parent`, `set_included_by_parent`
- **Program Assignment**: Associate customer programs that affect product availability: `view_customer_program_id`, `set_customer_program_id`

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| CatalogPermission | string | Permission constants for account catalog operations and visibility management.  Defines granular access control capabilities for catalog configuration including product visibility, inheritance rules, and program associations.   These permissions enable role-based access to catalog management functions within account hierarchies.  They are: - **Catalog Visibility**: Define which products are shown or hidden in this account's catalog: `view_show_in_catalog`, `set_show_in_catalog`, `view_hide_in_catalog`, `set_hide_in_catalog` - **Child Account Inheritance**: Set inclusion and exclusion rules that child accounts will inherit: `view_excluded_by_parent`, `set_excluded_by_parent`, `view_included_by_parent`, `set_included_by_parent` - **Program Assignment**: Associate customer programs that affect product availability: `view_customer_program_id`, `set_customer_program_id`  |  |

**Example**
<pre>set_show_in_catalog</pre>

#### CatalogOverridesConfig

Comprehensive account catalog configuration for product visibility and inheritance management.

Defines how products appear in account catalogs through multiple visibility layers including direct visibility controls, hierarchical inheritance rules, and program associations.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| excluded_by_parent | object | Products excluded from child account catalogs by parent configuration.  When enabled, child accounts cannot access these products regardless of other visibility settings. Inheritable setting that cascades through account hierarchies. <br>*Example:* `{"restricted-product-code":true,"internal-test-product":true}` | No |
| included_by_parent | object | Products explicitly included in child account catalogs by parent configuration.  Defines a whitelist of products available to child accounts. When configured, only listed products are accessible to descendants unless overridden. <br>*Example:* `{"amazon-us-gift-card":true,"starbucks-us-gift-card":true}` | No |
| show_in_catalog | object | Products explicitly visible in this account's catalog.  Direct visibility control for this specific account. Not inherited by child accounts, allowing account-specific catalog customization.  This list must still respect the inclusion list and exclusion list set by the parent account. <br>*Example:* `{"premium-product-code":true,"seasonal-promotion-card":true}` | No |
| hide_in_catalog | object | Products explicitly hidden from this account's catalog.  Direct visibility control that overrides inherited inclusions. Not inherited by child accounts, providing account-level customization.  This list must still respect the inclusion list and exclusion list set by the parent account. <br>*Example:* `{"competitor-brand-product":true,"deprecated-legacy-card":true}` | No |
| customer_program_id | string | Customer program identifier associated with this account for approval workflows.  Links the account to specific approval programs that determine product availability based on brand partnerships and compliance requirements. <br>*Example:* `"corporate-payouts-program-2024"` | No |

| assigned_catalog | [CatalogOverridesConfig](#catalogoverridesconfig) | Catalog configuration directly assigned to this account | No |
| inherited_catalog | [CatalogOverridesConfig](#catalogoverridesconfig) | Catalog configuration inherited from parent accounts | No |

#### ProductBase

Base product properties shared between complete product definitions and request payloads.

Contains essential product attributes including identification, classification, regional configuration, and internal metadata. Serves as the base schema for both product creation requests and complete product representations in the catalog system.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| shortcode | string | Unique product identifier used throughout the catalog system<br>*Example:* `"AMAZON-US-GIFT-CARD"` | No |
| type | [ProductType](#producttype) | Product type (e.g., open-loop, closed-loop) | No |
| currency | [Currency](#currency) | Currency (ISO 4217 currency code) | No |
| regions | [ [Region](#region) ] | Supported regions (ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 codes) | No |
| internal_display_name | string | Internal display name for the product | No |
| internal_description | string | Internal description of the product | No |
| internal_metadata | object | Internal metadata as JSON | No |
| name | string | Product name<br>*Example:* `"Gift Card"` | No |
| description | string | Detailed description of the product<br>*Example:* `"This gift card can be used to buy anything at the store."` | No |
| redemption_instructions | string | Instructions for redeeming the code<br>*Example:* `"Click here to redeem"` | No |
| terms_and_conditions | string | Terms and conditions<br>*Example:* `"You must be 18 years or older to redeem this code."` | No |
| disclaimer | string | Legal disclaimer or important notices for the product<br>*Example:* `"This product is not eligible for refunds."` | No |
| logo_image_url | string | URL to the product logo image<br>*Example:* `"https://www.example.com/logo.png"` | No |
| faceplate_image_url | string | URL to the product faceplate image<br>*Example:* `"https://www.example.com/faceplate.png"` | No |
| redemption_url | string | URL for product redemption<br>*Example:* `"https://www.example.com/redemption"` | No |
| active | boolean | Whether the product is active | No |

#### ApprovalProgramStatus

Status enumeration for approval program lifecycle tracking within brand partnership workflows.

Represents the current state of an organization's approval program application:
- **requested**: Initial application submitted by organization
- **pending**: Application under review by brand/supplier
- **approved**: Organization granted access to brand products
- **rejected**: Application denied by brand/supplier
- **cancelled**: Application withdrawn or program terminated

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| ApprovalProgramStatus | string | Status enumeration for approval program lifecycle tracking within brand partnership workflows.  Represents the current state of an organization's approval program application: - **requested**: Initial application submitted by organization - **pending**: Application under review by brand/supplier - **approved**: Organization granted access to brand products - **rejected**: Application denied by brand/supplier - **cancelled**: Application withdrawn or program terminated  |  |

**Example**
<pre>approved</pre>

#### ApprovalRequirement

Comprehensive approval requirement configuration for brand partnership and compliance workflows.

Defines the documentation, criteria, and processes needed for organizations to gain access to specific brand products. Includes approval guides, data requirements, supplier associations, and workflow parameters that govern brand partnership compliance across the catalog system.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| id | [UUID](#uuid) | Unique identifier for the approval requirement | No |
| name | string | Name of the approval requirement<br>*Example:* `"Amazon Brand Program"` | Yes |
| description | string | Description of the approval requirement<br>*Example:* `"Approval required for Amazon brand products"` | Yes |
| approval_guide | object | Guide for approval process (JSON object)<br>*Example:* `{"steps":["Complete application","Provide documentation"]}` | No |
| requires_data | boolean | Whether this approval requirement requires additional data<br>*Example:* `true` | No |
| supplier_id | [SupplierID](#supplierid) | Supplier ID this approval requirement belongs to | Yes |
| active | boolean | Whether this approval requirement is active<br>*Example:* `true` | No |
| created_time | dateTime | When the approval requirement was created | No |
| modified_time | dateTime | When the approval requirement was last modified | No |

Represents an organization's participation in a specific approval requirement, including application status, compliance data, metadata, and program hierarchy relationships.

#### ControlPermission

Standardized permission identifiers for account controls operations within the Lightrail platform.

These permissions define granular capabilities for managing financial and operational controls, enabling precise access control over what actions users can perform. Group permissions by operational area:

**Organization-Level Controls**: view/set_org_daily_limit
**Spending Controls**: view/set_daily_spend_limit, view/set_order_limit
**Transfer Controls**: view/set_daily_pull_from_parent_limit, view/set_daily_send_to_children_limit
**Payment Configuration**: view/set_payment_methods, view/set_base_currency
**Fee Management**: view/set_order_fees
**Revenue Sharing**: view/set_margin_share_*, view/set_fee_share_*, view/set_breakage_share_*
**Operational Settings**: view/set_default_order_value
**Flag Management**: view_account_flags, set_user_set_flags, delete_user_set_flags

All permissions follow the pattern of separate view and set capabilities, allowing fine-grained access control for compliance and security requirements.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| ControlPermission | string | Standardized permission identifiers for account controls operations within the Lightrail platform.  These permissions define granular capabilities for managing financial and operational controls, enabling precise access control over what actions users can perform. Group permissions by operational area:  **Organization-Level Controls**: view/set_org_daily_limit **Spending Controls**: view/set_daily_spend_limit, view/set_order_limit **Transfer Controls**: view/set_daily_pull_from_parent_limit, view/set_daily_send_to_children_limit **Payment Configuration**: view/set_payment_methods, view/set_base_currency **Fee Management**: view/set_order_fees **Revenue Sharing**: view/set_margin_share_*, view/set_fee_share_*, view/set_breakage_share_* **Operational Settings**: view/set_default_order_value **Flag Management**: view_account_flags, set_user_set_flags, delete_user_set_flags  All permissions follow the pattern of separate view and set capabilities, allowing fine-grained access control for compliance and security requirements.  |  |

**Example**
<pre>set_daily_spend_limit</pre>

#### ControlsConfig

Comprehensive account controls configuration structure defining financial and operational governance.

Provides the complete framework for account management including spending limits, transfer controls, payment configuration, fee structures, and revenue sharing arrangements. Each control can be individually enabled or disabled and supports multi-currency configuration where applicable.

Controls are organized into logical groups:
- **Organization-Level Controls**: Organization-wide spending limits and controls
- **Financial Limits**: Spending and transfer restrictions for risk management
- **Payment Configuration**: Approved methods and currency settings
- **Fee Structures**: Revenue optimization through fixed and percentage fees
- **Revenue Sharing**: Margin, fee, and breakage distribution across hierarchies
- **Operational Settings**: Default values and standard configurations

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| org_daily_limit | [OrgDailyLimitControl](#orgdailylimitcontrol) |  | No |
| org_daily_limit_override_from_parent | [OrgDailyLimitOverrideFromParentControl](#orgdailylimitoverridefromparentcontrol) |  | No |
| daily_pull_from_parent_limit | [DailyPullFromParentLimitControl](#dailypullfromparentlimitcontrol) |  | No |
| daily_spend_limit | [DailySpendLimitControl](#dailyspendlimitcontrol) |  | No |
| daily_send_to_children_limit | [DailySendToChildrenLimitControl](#dailysendtochildrenlimitcontrol) |  | No |
| order_limit | [OrderLimitControl](#orderlimitcontrol) |  | No |
| payment_methods | [PaymentMethodsControl](#paymentmethodscontrol) |  | No |
| base_currency | [BaseCurrencyControl](#basecurrencycontrol) |  | No |
| order_fees_fixed | [OrderFeesFixedControl](#orderfeesfixedcontrol) |  | No |
| order_fees_percentage | [OrderFeesPercentageControl](#orderfeespercentagecontrol) |  | No |
| discount_share_with_children | [DiscountShareWithChildrenControl](#discountsharewithchildrencontrol) |  | No |
| discount_share_override_from_parent | [DiscountShareOverrideFromParentControl](#discountshareoverridefromparentcontrol) |  | No |
| margin_share_with_children | [MarginShareWithChildrenControl](#marginsharewithchildrencontrol) |  | No |
| margin_share_override_from_parent | [MarginShareOverrideFromParentControl](#marginshareoverridefromparentcontrol) |  | No |
| fee_share_with_children | [FeeShareWithChildrenControl](#feesharewithchildrencontrol) |  | No |
| fee_share_override_from_parent | [FeeShareOverrideFromParentControl](#feeshareoverridefromparentcontrol) |  | No |
| breakage_share_with_children | [BreakageShareWithChildrenControl](#breakagesharewithchildrencontrol) |  | No |
| breakage_share_override_from_parent | [BreakageShareOverrideFromParentControl](#breakageshareoverridefromparentcontrol) |  | No |
| default_order_value | [DefaultOrderValueControl](#defaultordervaluecontrol) |  | No |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "org_daily_limit": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": {
      "USD": "10000.00",
      "EUR": "9000.00"
    }
  },
  "org_daily_limit_override_from_parent": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": {
      "USD": "10000.00",
      "EUR": "9000.00"
    }
  },
  "daily_spend_limit": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": {
      "USD": "5000.00",
      "EUR": "4500.00"
    }
  },
  "order_limit": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": {
      "USD": "1000.00",
      "EUR": "900.00"
    }
  },
  "payment_methods": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": [
      "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
      "11111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111"
    ]
  },
  "base_currency": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": "USD"
  },
  "order_fees_fixed": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": [
      {
        "id": "fee-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
        "amount": "2.50",
        "currency": "USD"
      }
    ]
  },
  "margin_share_with_children": {
    "enabled": true,
    "value": "0.15"
  }
}</pre>

#### OrderFeeFixed

Fixed amount fee structure for order processing charges.

Represents a specific fee with a predetermined amount and currency that is applied to orders. Each fee has a unique identifier enabling tracking, reporting, and management of different fee types such as processing charges, service fees, or administrative costs.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| OrderFeeFixed | object | Fixed amount fee structure for order processing charges.  Represents a specific fee with a predetermined amount and currency that is applied to orders. Each fee has a unique identifier enabling tracking, reporting, and management of different fee types such as processing charges, service fees, or administrative costs.  |  |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "id": "fee-processing-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
  "amount": "2.50",
  "currency": "USD"
}</pre>

#### OrderFeePercentage

Percentage-based fee structure calculated from order payout value.

Represents a dynamic fee that scales with the order amount, providing flexible revenue generation that adjusts to transaction sizes. Commonly used for commission structures, processing fees, and revenue sharing arrangements.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| id | string | Unique identifier for this specific percentage fee structure.  Used for tracking and managing different types of percentage-based fees such as commissions, processing fees, or revenue sharing arrangements. <br>*Example:* `"fee-commission-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"` | Yes |
| amount | [Rate](#rate) | Percentage rate applied to the order's payout value.  Expressed as a decimal (e.g., 0.025 = 2.5%). The fee amount is calculated by multiplying this rate by the order's payout value.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "id": "fee-commission-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
  "amount": "0.025"
}</pre>

#### CurrencyAmountControl

Flexible currency amount control supporting multi-currency limit configuration.

Provides the foundation for financial controls that need to specify different limits for different currencies. When enabled, requires currency-specific amounts to accommodate global operations and diverse payment scenarios.

Commonly used for spending limits, transfer restrictions, and order controls where different currencies may have varying risk profiles or business requirements.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether this financial control is actively enforced.  When false, the control is ignored and no limits are applied. When true, the specified currency amounts are enforced for all relevant transactions. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [CurrencyAmountMap](#currencyamountmap) | Currency-specific amount limits that apply when the control is enabled.  Each currency can have different limits to accommodate varying risk profiles, local regulations, or business requirements. All amounts use decimal string format for precision.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": {
    "USD": "5000.00",
    "EUR": "4500.00",
    "GBP": "4000.00"
  }
}</pre>

#### DailyPullFromParentLimitControl

Daily limit control for fund transfers from the parent account.

Restricts the total amount that can be transferred from the parent account per day, providing essential cash flow management and preventing unauthorized large transfers. This control is not inheritable as it governs the specific relationship between this account and its parent.

When enabled, all transfer requests from parent accounts are validated against daily totals. This control is crucial for managing liquidity, controlling cash flow, and maintaining proper fund governance across account hierarchies.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| DailyPullFromParentLimitControl |  | Daily limit control for fund transfers from the parent account.  Restricts the total amount that can be transferred from the parent account per day, providing essential cash flow management and preventing unauthorized large transfers. This control is not inheritable as it governs the specific relationship between this account and its parent.  When enabled, all transfer requests from parent accounts are validated against daily totals. This control is crucial for managing liquidity, controlling cash flow, and maintaining proper fund governance across account hierarchies.  |  |

#### DailySpendLimitControl

Daily spending limit control for orders purchased directly through the account.

Enforces maximum daily spending amounts across all currencies to manage financial risk and ensure compliance with organizational policies. This control is inheritable, allowing parent accounts to set spending policies that cascade to child accounts unless explicitly overridden.

When enabled, all direct orders from this account are validated against the daily spending totals. The limit resets at midnight UTC and applies to the total value of all orders placed, regardless of payment method or product type.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| DailySpendLimitControl |  | Daily spending limit control for orders purchased directly through the account.  Enforces maximum daily spending amounts across all currencies to manage financial risk and ensure compliance with organizational policies. This control is inheritable, allowing parent accounts to set spending policies that cascade to child accounts unless explicitly overridden.  When enabled, all direct orders from this account are validated against the daily spending totals. The limit resets at midnight UTC and applies to the total value of all orders placed, regardless of payment method or product type.  |  |

#### OrgDailyLimitOverrideFromParentControl

Daily limit override control for organization-wide spending.

Allows a parent account to override the daily spending limit on a per account basis. When enabled, the daily spending limit is set to the value specified in the value field for this account and all child accounts.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| OrgDailyLimitOverrideFromParentControl |  | Daily limit override control for organization-wide spending.  Allows a parent account to override the daily spending limit on a per account basis. When enabled, the daily spending limit is set to the value specified in the value field for this account and all child accounts.  |  |

#### OrgDailyLimitControl

Daily limit control for organization-wide spending.

Restricts the total amount that can be spent by the organization per day, providing essential financial governance and preventing unauthorized large spending. 

This control is inheritable, allowing parent accounts to set spending policies that cascade to child accounts and can only be set on the top level account of an organization.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| OrgDailyLimitControl |  | Daily limit control for organization-wide spending.  Restricts the total amount that can be spent by the organization per day, providing essential financial governance and preventing unauthorized large spending.   This control is inheritable, allowing parent accounts to set spending policies that cascade to child accounts and can only be set on the top level account of an organization.  |  |

#### DailySendToChildrenLimitControl

Daily limit control for funding orders of children accounts.

Sets aggregate daily limits for funding orders of children accounts, helping manage cash flow and prevent excessive fund distribution. This control is not inheritable as it governs the specific distribution relationship between this account and its children.

When enabled, the sum of all funding orders of children accounts is tracked and validated against these daily limits. This provides necessary oversight for fund distribution and helps maintain proper capital allocation across the account hierarchy.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| DailySendToChildrenLimitControl |  | Daily limit control for funding orders of children accounts.  Sets aggregate daily limits for funding orders of children accounts, helping manage cash flow and prevent excessive fund distribution. This control is not inheritable as it governs the specific distribution relationship between this account and its children.  When enabled, the sum of all funding orders of children accounts is tracked and validated against these daily limits. This provides necessary oversight for fund distribution and helps maintain proper capital allocation across the account hierarchy.  |  |

#### OrderLimitControl

Per-order limit control for individual orders from the account.

Sets maximum allowable amounts for individual orders to prevent large unauthorized orders and manage per-transaction risk exposure. This control is inheritable and can be used to implement graduated spending authority across account hierarchies.

When enabled, each order is validated against these limits before processing. This provides fine-grained control over order sizes and helps prevent fraud or errors involving large amounts.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| OrderLimitControl |  | Per-order limit control for individual orders from the account.  Sets maximum allowable amounts for individual orders to prevent large unauthorized orders and manage per-transaction risk exposure. This control is inheritable and can be used to implement graduated spending authority across account hierarchies.  When enabled, each order is validated against these limits before processing. This provides fine-grained control over order sizes and helps prevent fraud or errors involving large amounts.  |  |

#### PaymentMethodsControl

Payment methods restriction control for account orders.

Defines which payment methods are available for use within this account, providing essential security and compliance controls. This control is inheritable, allowing organizations to set payment policies at parent levels that cascade to child accounts.

When enabled, only the specified payment methods can be used for orders. This enables compliance with payment card industry standards, fraud prevention, and organizational payment policies.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether payment method restrictions are actively enforced.  When false, all available payment methods are permitted. When true, only the specified payment methods in the value array are allowed for orders. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [ [UUID](#uuid) ] | List of approved payment method identifiers that can be used for orders.  Each identifier corresponds to a configured payment method in the system. Only these methods will be available for order processing when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": [
    "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
    "11111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111"
  ]
}</pre>

#### BaseCurrencyControl

Base currency designation control for account orders.

Establishes the primary currency for account orders, reporting, and default order processing. This control is inheritable and provides essential standardization across account hierarchies for financial reporting and operational consistency.

When enabled, the specified currency becomes the default for new orders, fee calculations, and financial reporting. This simplifies multi-currency operations and ensures consistent accounting practices.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether base currency standardization is actively enforced.  When false, orders can use any supported currency. When true, the specified base currency is used as the default for operations and reporting. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Currency](#currency) | Primary currency code for account orders.  This currency will be used as the default for new orders, fee calculations, and financial reporting when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "USD"
}</pre>

#### OrderFeesFixedControl

Fixed amount order fees control for revenue optimization.

Enables charging predetermined fixed fees on orders placed by accounts lower in the hierarchy. These fees are added to the order total and provide a mechanism for parent accounts to generate revenue from child account activity.

This control is not inheritable as fee structures are typically managed at specific hierarchy levels. Multiple fees can be configured with different currencies and amounts to support diverse business models and geographical requirements.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether fixed order fees are actively charged.  When false, no additional fixed fees are applied to orders. When true, the specified fees are added to all qualifying orders from the account and its child accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [ [OrderFeeFixed](#orderfeefixed) ] | List of fixed fee structures to apply to the account and its child accounts.  Each fee includes a unique identifier, fixed amount, and currency. All specified fees are applied to orders, allowing for complex fee structures including service charges, processing fees, and markup amounts.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": [
    {
      "id": "fee-processing-00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
      "amount": "2.50",
      "currency": "USD"
    },
    {
      "id": "fee-service-11111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111",
      "amount": "5.00",
      "currency": "USD"
    }
  ]
}</pre>

#### OrderFeesPercentageControl

Percentage-based order fees control for order fee processing.

Enables charging fees as a percentage of the order value for the account and its child accounts. This provides dynamic revenue scaling that adjusts with order sizes and supports percentage-based business models.

This control is not inheritable as percentage fee structures require careful configuration at specific hierarchy levels. Multiple percentage fees can be configured to support complex business models including commission structures and revenue sharing agreements.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether percentage-based order fees are actively charged.  When false, no percentage fees are applied to orders. When true, the specified percentage fees are calculated and added to all qualifying orders from the account and its child accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [ [OrderFeePercentage](#orderfeepercentage) ] | List of percentage fee structures to apply to the account and its child accounts.  Each fee includes a unique identifier and percentage rate. Fees are calculated as a percentage of the order's payout value and added to the total order amount.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": [
    {
      "id": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
      "amount": "0.025"
    },
    {
      "id": "11111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111",
      "amount": "0.015"
    }
  ]
}</pre>

#### DiscountShareWithChildrenControl

Discount sharing control for distributing product discounts to child accounts at the time of order for standard payouts.

Configures what percentage of product discount (from face value) is shared with child accounts in the hierarchy.

This control is not inheritable as discount sharing requires explicit configuration for each level of the hierarchy. The shared discount becomes available as additional discount or credit for child accounts when they place orders.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether discount sharing with children accounts is active.  When false, no discount is shared and any product discount available is retained by this account. When true, the specified percentage of available discount is shared with children accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Percentage of product discount to share with children accounts.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.15 = 15%). This percentage of the product discount is made available to children accounts as additional savings or credit.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.15"
}</pre>

#### DiscountShareOverrideFromParentControl

Discount share override control for customizing parent account revenue sharing.

Allows a parent account to override the discount sharing rate on a per account basis. When enabled, discounts will be shared to this account with this rate instead of the parent's share with children setting.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether the parent discount share override is active.  When false, discount will be shared with this account using the parent's discount sharing rate. When true, the parent will share discount with this account using the rate specified in the value field. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Custom discount share percentage that overrides the rate set by parent to this account.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.10 = 10%). This rate is used instead of the rate set by parent to this account when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### MarginShareWithChildrenControl

Margin sharing control for distributing product discounts to child accounts.

Configures what percentage of product margin (discount from face value) is shared with child accounts in the hierarchy.

This control is not inheritable as margin sharing requires explicit configuration for each level of the hierarchy. The shared margin becomes available as additional discount or credit for child accounts when they place orders.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether margin sharing with children accounts is active.  When false, no margin is shared and the full product discount is retained by this account. When true, the specified percentage of margin is shared with children accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Percentage of product margin to share with children accounts.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.15 = 15%). This percentage of the product discount is made available to children accounts as additional savings or credit.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.15"
}</pre>

#### MarginShareOverrideFromParentControl

Margin share override control for customizing parent account revenue sharing.

Allows this account to override the margin sharing rate inherited from parent accounts. When enabled, uses a custom rate instead of the parent's setting.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether margin share override is actively enforced.  When false, inherits the parent's margin sharing rate. When true, uses the custom override rate specified in the value field. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Custom margin share percentage that overrides the rate set by parent to this account.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.10 = 10%). This rate is used instead of the rate set by parent to this account when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### FeeShareWithChildrenControl

Fee sharing control for distributing fee revenue to children accounts.

Configures what percentage of fee revenue is shared with children accounts in the hierarchy.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether fee sharing with children accounts is active.  When false, no fees are shared with children accounts. When true, the specified percentage of fee revenue is distributed to children accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Percentage of fee revenue to share with children accounts.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.20 = 20%). This percentage of fee revenue is distributed to children accounts when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### FeeShareOverrideFromParentControl

Fee share override control for customizing rate set by parent to this account.

Allows this account to override the rate set by parent to this account. When enabled, uses a custom rate instead of the rate set by parent to this account.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether fee share override is actively enforced.  When false, inherits the rate set by parent to this account. When true, uses the custom override rate specified in the value field. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Custom fee share percentage that overrides the rate set by parent to this account.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.15 = 15%). This rate is used instead of the rate set by parent to this account when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### BreakageShareWithChildrenControl

Breakage sharing control for distributing unclaimed value revenue to children accounts.

Configures what percentage of breakage revenue from expired or unclaimed products is shared with children accounts.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether breakage sharing with children accounts is active.  When false, no breakage revenue is shared with children accounts. When true, the specified percentage of breakage revenue is distributed to children accounts. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Percentage of breakage revenue to share with children accounts.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.25 = 25%). This percentage of revenue from expired or unclaimed products is distributed to children accounts.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### BreakageShareOverrideFromParentControl

Breakage share override control for customizing rate set by parent to this account.

Allows this account to override the rate set by parent to this account. When enabled, uses a custom rate instead of the rate set by parent to this account.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether breakage share override is actively enforced.  When false, inherits the rate set by parent to this account. When true, uses the custom override rate specified in the value field. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [Rate](#rate) | Custom breakage share percentage that overrides the rate set by parent to this account.  Expressed as a decimal rate (e.g., 0.18 = 18%). This rate is used instead of the rate set by parent to this account when the control is enabled.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": "0.05"
}</pre>

#### DefaultOrderValueControl

Default order value control for standardizing order amounts.

Sets a standard default amount and currency for new orders to streamline the ordering process and provide consistent user experience. This control is inheritable, allowing organizations to establish standard order amounts across account hierarchies.

When enabled, the specified amount and currency are pre-populated in order forms and interfaces, reducing user input requirements and promoting standardized transaction sizes that align with business objectives.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| enabled | boolean | Whether default order value standardization is active.  When false, no default values are pre-populated in order interfaces. When true, the specified amount and currency are used as defaults for new orders. <br>*Example:* `true` | Yes |
| value | [AmountWithCurrency](#amountwithcurrency) | Standard default amount and currency for new orders with this account.  This value will be pre-populated in order interfaces when the control is enabled, providing consistency and reducing user input requirements.  | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "enabled": true,
  "value": {
    "currency": "USD",
    "amount": "250.00"
  }
}</pre>

#### GetAccountControlsSuccessBody

Response containing the complete controls configuration for an account, including both assigned and inherited settings.

Provides comprehensive visibility into the account's control landscape for governance, compliance, and operational management.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| assigned_controls | [ControlsConfig](#controlsconfig) | Controls directly configured on this specific account.  These controls are managed explicitly for this account and can be modified through the controls configuration endpoint. They take precedence over inherited controls for the same control types.  | No |
| inherited_controls | [ControlsConfig](#controlsconfig) | Controls inherited from parent accounts in the hierarchy.  These controls cannot be modified at this account level but contribute to the effective control set. They apply when no corresponding assigned control overrides them.  | No |

#### GetAccountFlagsSuccessBody

Response containing all configuration flags currently active for an account including both applied and inherited settings.

Provides complete flag visibility for account behavior control, security management, and operational status oversight. Includes flag inheritance hierarchy for comprehensive access management and administrative configuration tracking.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| applied_flags | [ [AccountFlags](#accountflags) ] | Array of account configuration flags applied to this account controlling operational behavior and security settings | Yes |
| inherited_flags | [ [AccountFlags](#accountflags) ] | Array of account configuration flags inherited from parent accounts controlling operational behavior and security settings | Yes |

**Example**
<pre>{
  "applied_flags": [
    "user_paused"
  ],
  "inherited_flags": [
    "admin_trusted"
  ]
}</pre>

#### SupplierPermission

Permission constants for internal supplier integration operations.

Defines specific capabilities required for managing supplier partnerships, encryption key operations, and secure product fulfillment processes.

| Name | Type | Description | Required |
| ---- | ---- | ----------- | -------- |
| SupplierPermission | string | Permission constants for internal supplier integration operations.  Defines specific capabilities required for managing supplier partnerships, encryption key operations, and secure product fulfillment processes.  |  |

**Example**
<pre>rotate_code_encryption_key</pre>
